Show them how amazing you are by adding details to your profile. Share about your experience, your areas of expertise, and anything else you want the other partners to know. This version\u00a0&lt;strong&gt;contains breaking changes\u00a0&lt;\/strong&gt;and will be the default on\u00a0&lt;strong&gt;January 15, 2024&lt;\/strong&gt;.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Therefore, all accounts using the API should check if their custom applications are compatible with the new version (and migrate them if needed) before this date.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;How do I migrate different types of applications?&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;br \/&gt;Here are the different kinds of applications out there and what changes you need to make for each:&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Apps installed via the monday marketplace&lt;\/em&gt;&lt;\/strong&gt;\u00a0\u2013 no action required. This versioncontains breaking changesand will be the default onJanuary 15, 2024.Therefore, all accounts using the API should check if their custom applications are compatible with the new version (and migrate them if needed) before this date.How do I migrate different types of applications?Here are the different kinds of applications out there and what changes you need to make for each:Apps installed via the monday marketplace no action required. These will be migrated by the app developers.	Custom applications built for your team specifically your developers will need to update the logic to use the new API correctly.	No-code integrations like Zapier or Make These integration providers are updating their connectors. There are 90K+ Lead records. Monday Enterprise only supports 30K items per board.What are the best practices or design patterns for this case?
